Coding\n\n你是一个在持续运行的智能体的一部分，你的工作是在工作空间中提取当前优先级最高的未完成的任务，并且完成它。注意，在你开始运行之时，你具有干净的上下文，没有关于这个项目的任何信息，你需要通过查看工作目录来获取项目的整体面貌和你的任务。\n\n### 第一步：查看工程目录，并且了解当前项目的主要信息\n\n你可以通过查看下面的文件来查看你当前需要做什么：\n\n```bash\n# 1. 查看你当前的工作目录\npwd\n\n# 2. 查看当前目录下的所有文件来理解当前项目的结构\nls -la\n\n# 3. 从当前目录中读取需求文档来了解当前项目的完整需求\ncat app_spec.md\n\n# 4. 从tasks.json文件中来查看你当前需要执行的任务\ncat tasks.json | head -50\n\n# 5. 读取过程文件来查看之前的其他合作者们做了什么\ncat progress.txt\n\n# 6. 从git log中查看其他合作者们最近做了什么\ngit log --online -20\n\n# 7. 查询当前还有多少未完成的任务\ncat tasks.json | grep '\"passes\": false' | wc -l\n```\n\n**注意：**理解`app_spec.md`是非常重要的，它包含了关于这个项目的所有需求信息！\n\n### 第二步：选择一个你将要实现的任务\n\n你需要从`tasks.json`文件中选取一个任务并且执行它，这个文件中所有的任务都是按照优先级排序的，你需要选择一个具有最高优先级的任务然后完成它。\n\n每一个任务都有一个\"passes\"标签，你要选择一passes标签值为`false`的任务来完成它。\n\n**注意：**千万不要贪多！在这个阶段，你只需要选择1个你将要完成的任务即可，无需选择更多任务来完成！\n\n\n### 第三步：实现你选择的任务\n\n现在，你已经选择了一个任务，接下来你需要在项目中进行代码书写来完成这个任务，你可以按照下面的步骤来执行：\n\n1. 查看当前任务的`description`字段，结合你对`app_spec.md`的查看，来理解当前需要实现的具体功能\n2. 在项目中书写代码来实现当前功能\n3. 按照`steps`字段规定的测试步骤对你的功能进行严格测试\n4. 如果有任何测试结果不符合预期的地方，你需要解决它并重新测试\n5. 确保测试结果完美符合预期\n\n**重要：**这一步完成的唯一标志是你书写完了代码，并且成功通过测试且完美符合预期。你必须在完成工作的过程中在终端中向用户详细展示你正在做什么，遇到了哪些问题，以及你打算怎么解决等。\n\n#### IMPORTANT\n\nFor web applications, you MUST verify features through thr actual UI, you can use the playwright MCP to do this.\n\n**DO:**\n- Test through the UI with clicks and keyboard input\n- Take screenshots to verify visual appearance\n- Check for console errors in browser\n- Verify complete user workflows end-to-end\n\n**DON'T:**\n- Only test with curl commands (backend testing alone is insufficient)\n- Use JavaScript evaluation to bypass UI (no shortcuts)\n- Skip visual verification\n- Mark tests passing without thorough verification\n\n### 第四步：更新`tasks.json`（万分小心！）\n\n#### 注意：你是一个无情的执行者，你无权对任务本身做任何删减和更改，也不要擅自添加新的任务进去，你唯一可以编辑的字段是你选中的那个任务的`passes`字段！\n\n在你完成了你选中的任务并且成功通过测试之后，你可以对你选中的任务做如下修改：\n\n```json\n\"passes\": false\n```\n\n改成:\n\n```json\n\"passes\": true\n```\n\n#### 修改完之后你需要做下面的事情\n\n将当前任务移动到任务列表的末尾，然后将新的json内容重新写入`tasks.json`文件，这一步也很重要，因为这会保证任何Agent开始运行之后，最重要的那个任务永远在文件开头。\n\n### 第五步：更新过程文件(万分小心)\n\n#### 注意：`progress.txt`文件里的内容记录了当前项目所有的开发记录，你万万不能对`progress.txt`文件中已有的内容做任何修改。你只要将你需要添加的内容添加到原有文件内容的开头即可。\n\n下面是你需要添加的内容：\n\n1. 你完成了哪一个任务\n2. 你做了哪些测试\n3. 你发现并解决了哪些问题？如何解决的？\n4. 你建议下一步应该做什么?\n5. 当前工程完成的状态(如: \"20个测试通过，共47个测试\")\n\n你可以通过下面的命令将你要添加的内容添加到`progress.txt`文件里:\n\n```bash\nsed -i '1i [你将要添加的内容]\\n\\n'\n```\n\n#### IMPORTANT\n- **NEVER COVER THE ORIGINAL CONTENTS IN PROGRESS.TXT.** Just simply insert your new contents at the start of the file.\n\n### 第六步：提交你的工作\n\n通过git提交你的工作，详细描述你在当前提交中做了什么:\n\n```bash\ngit add .\ngit commit -m \"实现了[功能名称],并完成了测试\n\n - 添加了哪些改动\n - 更新了tasks.json: 完成了[功能名称]功能的测试\n - 测试相关截图在 verification/[directory]文件夹下\n\"\n```\n\n\n**注意：**你是一个无情的执行者，你没有权力对任务本身的合理性进行任何的质疑和评价，你只需要将当前具有最高优先级且未完成的任务拿出来，并且完成它。你有无限多的时间来完成这些任务，因此不必担心时间不够用，对你唯一的考核就是严格完成你选中的任务并且完成它即可，我不需要你完成的有多快，但要求你必须完成地足够完美！\n\n"}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"67eb63cd-4a2e-4a6a-a04b-2cd0f727c6de","uuid":"6abd9fcd-e024-4b9f-aeed-b477407edc36","isSynthetic":true}

{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"call_1f0a4aed146e4eb994ce4016","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→```xml\n     2→<project_specification>\n     3→  <project_name>Image Detection Result Analyzer - Frontend Tool</project_name>\n     4→\n     5→  <overview>\n     6→    Build a comprehensive frontend tool with a Flask backend to analyze the performance of object detection models by comparing ground truth annotations with model predictions. The application will process local datasets consisting of image sequences, ground truth bounding box JSON files, and model prediction JSON files (containing bounding boxes, classes, and confidence scores). It provides two core views: a statistics dashboard displaying per-class detection metrics (recall, false positive rate, etc.) and an image-by-image comparison view showing visual overlays of ground truth and predicted bounding boxes with distinct visual indicators for correct detections, false positives, and missed detections. The tool prioritizes intuitive visualization, accurate metric calculation, and seamless local file handling.\n     7→  </overview>\n     8→\n     9→  <technology_stack>\n    10→    <frontend>\n    11→      <framework>Vanilla HTML5, CSS3, JavaScript (ES6+)</framework>\n    12→      <styling>Custom CSS with Flexbox/Grid, optional Bootstrap 5 (via CDN) for responsive layout</styling>\n    13→      <visualization>Chart.js (CDN) for statistical charts, Canvas API for bounding box rendering</visualization>\n    14→      <file_handling>FileReader API for local file processing</file_handling>\n    15→      <routing>Client-side routing with JavaScript (hash-based) for page navigation</routing>\n    16→      <icons>Font Awesome (CDN) for visual indicators (check, cross, dash)</icons>\n    17→    </frontend>\n    18→    <backend>\n    19→      <runtime>Python 3.8+</runtime>\n    20→      <framework>Flask 2.0+</framework>\n    21→      <data_processing>\n    22→        - JSON parsing with built-in json module\n    23→        - Image processing with Pillow (PIL) for thumbnail generation\n    24→        - Metric calculation (recall, precision, FPR) with numpy\n    25→      </data_processing>\n    26→      <cors>Flask-CORS for cross-origin resource sharing</cors>\n    27→      <file_management>Built-in os/pathlib for local file system interaction</file_management>\n    28→    </backend>\n    29→    <communication>\n    30→      <api>RESTful endpoints for data processing and retrieval</api>\n    31→      <data_format>JSON for all data exchange between frontend and backend</data_format>\n    32→      <file_upload>Multipart/form-data for batch file upload (optional) or local file path specification</file_handling>\n    33→    </communication>\n    34→    <dependencies>\n    35→      <python>\n    36→        - Bootstrap 5.3.0 (optional)\n    44→        - Font Awesome 6.4.0\n    45→      </frontend_cdn>\n    46→    </dependencies>\n    47→  </technology_stack>\n    48→\n    49→  <prerequisites>\n    50→    <environment_setup>\n    51→      - Python 3.8+ installed on the system\n    52→      - Flask and required dependencies installed via pip: pip install flask flask-cors pillow numpy\n    53→      - Local dataset organized in a structured directory (images in /images, ground truth JSON in /gt, predictions JSON in /predictions)\n    54→      - Backend code in /app directory with app.py as entry point\n    55→      - Frontend assets (HTML/CSS/JS) in /app/static directory\n    56→      - Template files in /app/templates directory\n    57→      - All images in a single directory (JPG/PNG format) with consistent naming convention (e.g., img_001.jpg, img_002.png)\n    62→        - Image dimensions consistent or variable (tool should handle both)\n    63→      </image_sequence>\n    64→      <ground_truth_json>\n    65→        - Single JSON file or per-image JSON files (naming matching images: img_001.json)\n    66→        - Structure: {\n    67→            \"filename\": \"img_001.jpg\",\n    68→            \"width\": 1920,\n    69→            \"height\": 1080,\n    70→            \"annotations\": [\n    71→              {\n    72→                \"class\": \"car\",\n    73→                \"bbox\": [x1, y1, x2, y2]  # pixel coordinates (top-left, bottom-right)\n    74→              },\n    75→              ...\n    76→            ]\n    77→          }\n    78→      </ground_truth_json>\n    79→      <prediction_json>\n    80→        - Single JSON file or per-image JSON files (naming matching images: img_001_pred.json)\n    81→        - Structure: {\n    82→            \"filename\": \"img_001.jpg\",\n    83→            \"width\": 1920,\n    84→            \"height\": 1080,\n    85→            \"predictions\": [\n    86→              {\n    87→                \"class\": \"car\",\n    88→                \"bbox\": [x1, y1, x2, y2],\n    89→                \"score\": 0.95  # confidence score (0-1)\n    90→              },\n    91→              ...\n    92→            ]\n    93→          }\n    94→      </prediction_json>\n    95→    </dataset_format>\n    96→  </prerequisites>\n    97→\n    98→  <core_features>\n    99→    <file_handling>\n   100→      - Local dataset path configuration (input field for directory path)\n   101→      - Validation of dataset structure (check for images, GT JSON, prediction JSON)\n   102→      - Batch parsing of all files in the dataset directory\n   103→      - Error handling for missing files, invalid JSON formats, and mismatched filenames\n   104→      - Thumbnail generation for all images (150x150px, aspect ratio preserved)\n   105→      - Caching of parsed data to avoid reprocessing on page refresh\n   106→    </file_handling>\n   107→\n   108→    <statistics_dashboard>\n   109→      <metrics_calculation>\n   110→        - **Recall (True Positive Rate)**: TP / (TP + FN) per class\n   111→        - **Precision**: TP / (TP + FP) per class\n   112→        - **False Positive Rate (FPR)**: FP / (FP + TN) per class\n   113→        - **F1 Score**: 2 * (Precision * Recall) / (Precision + Recall) per class\n   114→        - **Overall Accuracy**: (TP + TN) / (TP + TN + FP + FN)\n   115→        - **Average Precision (AP)** per class (optional)\n   116→        - **Intersection over Union (IoU)** threshold configuration (default: 0.5) for TP/FP/FN classification\n   117→      </metrics_calculation>\n   118→      <visualization>\n   119→        - Bar charts for per-class recall, precision, FPR\n   120→        - Pie charts for class distribution in ground truth vs predictions\n   121→        - Summary table with all metrics for easy comparison\n   122→        - Sortable and filterable metric table (by class name, metric value)\n   123→        - Export statistics to CSV/JSON format\n   124→        - Interactive tooltips on charts showing exact metric values\n   125→      </visualization>\n   126→      <user_interface>\n   127→        - Dropdown for IoU threshold adjustment (0.3 to 0.9 in 0.1 increments)\n   128→        - Class filter (show/hide specific classes in charts/tables)\n   129→        - Confidence score threshold filter for predictions (0.0 to 1.0 slider)\n   130→        - Reset filters button to restore default settings\n   131→        - Summary card with key overall metrics (total images, total classes, average recall/precision)\n   132→      </user_interface>\n   133→    </statistics_dashboard>\n   134→\n   135→    <image_comparison_view>\n   136→      <left_panel>\n   137→        - Highlight active/selected image in the list\n   141→        - Pagination (optional) for large datasets (10/20/50 images per page)\n   142→        - Class filter (show only images containing specific classes)\n   143→        - Status filter (show only images with FP/FN/perfect detections)\n   144→      </left_panel>\n   145→      <right_panel>\n   146→        <image_display>\n   147→          - High-resolution image view (scaled to fit viewport, maintain aspect ratio)\n   148→          - Interactive canvas overlay for bounding boxes\n   149→          - Bounding box styles:\n   150→            - True Positive (TP): Green border (2px), green checkmark (✓) at top-left corner\n   151→            - False Positive (FP): Red border (2px), red cross (✗) at top-left corner\n   152→            - False Negative (FN): Red border (2px), red horizontal dash (—) at top-left corner\n   153→          - Bounding box labels (class name + confidence score for predictions)\n   154→          - The application will process local datasets consisting of image sequences, ground truth bounding box JSON files, and model prediction JSON files (containing bounding boxes, classes, and confidence scores). It provides two core views: a statistics dashboard displaying per-class detection metrics (recall, false positive rate, etc.) and an image-by-image comparison view showing visual overlays of ground truth and predicted bounding boxes with distinct visual indicators for correct detections, false positives, and missed detections. The tool prioritizes intuitive visualization, accurate metric calculation, and seamless local file handling.\n  </overview>\n\n  <technology_stack>\n    <frontend>\n      <framework>Vanilla HTML5, CSS3, JavaScript (ES6+)</framework>\n      <styling>Custom CSS with Flexbox/Grid, optional Bootstrap 5 (via CDN) for responsive layout</styling>\n      <visualization>Chart.js (CDN) for statistical charts, Canvas API for bounding box rendering</visualization>\n      <file_handling>FileReader API for local file processing</file_handling>\n      <routing>Client-side routing with JavaScript (hash-based) for page navigation</routing>\n      <icons>Font Awesome (CDN) for visual indicators (check, cross, dash)</icons>\n    </frontend>\n    <backend>\n      <runtime>Python 3.8+</runtime>\n      <framework>Flask 2.0+</framework>\n      <data_processing>\n        - JSON parsing with built-in json module\n        - Image processing with Pillow (PIL) for thumbnail generation\n        - Metric calculation (recall, precision, FPR) with numpy\n      </data_processing>\n      <cors>Flask-CORS for cross-origin resource sharing</cors>\n      <file_management>Built-in os/pathlib for local file system interaction</file_management>\n    </backend>\n    <communication>\n      <api>RESTful endpoints for data processing and retrieval</api>\n      <data_format>JSON for all data exchange between frontend and backend</data_format>\n      <file_upload>Multipart/form-data for batch file upload (optional) or local file path specification</file_handling>\n    </communication>\n    <dependencies>\n      <python>\n        - flask>=2.0.0\n        - flask-cors>=3.0.10\n        - pillow>=9.0.0\n        - numpy>=1.21.0\n      </python>\n      <frontend_cdn>\n        - Chart.js v4.4.0\n        - Bootstrap 5.3.0 (optional)\n        - Font Awesome 6.4.0\n      </frontend_cdn>\n    </dependencies>\n  </technology_stack>\n\n  <prerequisites>\n    <environment_setup>\n      - Python 3.8+ installed on the system\n      - Flask and required dependencies installed via pip: pip install flask flask-cors pillow numpy\n      - Local dataset organized in a structured directory (images in /images, ground truth JSON in /gt, predictions JSON in /predictions)\n      - Backend code in /app directory with app.py as entry point\n      - Frontend assets (HTML/CSS/JS) in /app/static directory\n      - Template files in /app/templates directory\n      - Environment variables (optional) for dataset path configuration (.env file with DATASET_PATH)\n    </environment_setup>\n    <dataset_format>\n      <image_sequence>\n        - All images in a single directory (JPG/PNG format) with consistent naming convention (e.g., img_001.jpg, img_002.png)\n        - Image dimensions consistent or variable (tool should handle both)\n      </image_sequence>\n      <ground_truth_json>\n        - Single JSON file or per-image JSON files (naming matching images: img_001.json)\n        - Structure: {\n            \"filename\": \"img_001.jpg\",\n            \"width\": 1920,\n            \"height\": 1080,\n            \"annotations\": [\n              {\n                \"class\": \"car\",\n                \"bbox\": [x1, y1, x2, y2]  # pixel coordinates (top-left, bottom-right)\n              },\n              ...\n            ]\n          }\n      </ground_truth_json>\n      <prediction_json>\n        - Single JSON file or per-image JSON files (naming matching images: img_001_pred.json)\n        - Structure: {\n            \"filename\": \"img_001.jpg\",\n            \"width\": 1920,\n            \"height\": 1080,\n            \"predictions\": [\n              {\n                \"class\": \"car\",\n                \"bbox\": [x1, y1, x2, y2],\n                \"score\": 0.95  # confidence score (0-1)\n              },\n              ...\n            ]\n          }\n      </prediction_json>\n    </dataset_format>\n  </prerequisites>\n\n  <core_features>\n    <file_handling>\n      - Local dataset path configuration (input field for directory path)\n      - Validation of dataset structure (check for images, GT JSON, prediction JSON)\n      - Batch parsing of all files in the dataset directory\n      - Error handling for missing files, invalid JSON formats, and mismatched filenames\n      - Thumbnail generation for all images (150x150px, aspect ratio preserved)\n      - Caching of parsed data to avoid reprocessing on page refresh\n    </file_handling>\n\n    <statistics_dashboard>\n      <metrics_calculation>\n        - **Recall (True Positive Rate)**: TP / (TP + FN) per class\n        - **Precision**: TP / (TP + FP) per class\n        - **False Positive Rate (FPR)**: FP / (FP + TN) per class\n        - **F1 Score**: 2 * (Precision * Recall) / (Precision + Recall) per class\n        - **Overall Accuracy**: (TP + TN) / (TP + TN + FP + FN)\n        - **Average Precision (AP)** per class (optional)\n        - **Intersection over Union (IoU)** threshold configuration (default: 0.5) for TP/FP/FN classification\n      </metrics_calculation>\n      <visualization>\n        - Bar charts for per-class recall, precision, FPR\n        - Pie charts for class distribution in ground truth vs predictions\n        - Summary table with all metrics for easy comparison\n        - Sortable and filterable metric table (by class name, metric value)\n        - Export statistics to CSV/JSON format\n        - Interactive tooltips on charts showing exact metric values\n      </visualization>\n      <user_interface>\n        - Dropdown for IoU threshold adjustment (0.3 to 0.9 in 0.1 increments)\n        - Class filter (show/hide specific classes in charts/tables)\n        - Confidence score threshold filter for predictions (0.0 to 1.0 slider)\n        - Reset filters button to restore default settings\n        - Summary card with key overall metrics (total images, total classes, average recall/precision)\n      </user_interface>\n    </statistics_dashboard>\n\n    <image_comparison_view>\n      <left_panel>\n        - Searchable and filterable file list (by filename, class presence)\n        - Image thumbnails alongside filenames (150x150px)\n        - Scrollable list with fixed height (occupies 100% of viewport height)\n        - Highlight active/selected image in the list\n        - Pagination (optional) for large datasets (10/20/50 images per page)\n        - Class filter (show only images containing specific classes)\n        - Status filter (show only images with FP/FN/perfect detections)\n      </left_panel>\n      <right_panel>\n        <image_display>\n          - High-resolution image view (scaled to fit viewport, maintain aspect ratio)\n          - Interactive canvas overlay for bounding boxes\n          - Bounding box styles:\n            - True Positive (TP): Green border (2px), green checkmark (✓) at top-left corner\n            - False Positive (FP): Red border (2px), red cross (✗) at top-left corner\n            - False Negative (FN): Red border (2px), red horizontal dash (—) at top-left corner\n          - Bounding box labels (class name + confidence score for predictions)\n          - Zoom/pan functionality for detailed inspection\n          - Toggle visibility of ground truth/prediction boxes\n          - Toggle visibility of box labels/indicators\n        </image_display>\n        <per_image_statistics>\n          - Summary card for current image (filename, dimensions, total GT boxes, total predicted boxes)\n          - Per-class breakdown table (GT count, predicted count, TP, FP, FN for each class)\n          - IoU values for each matched bounding box (optional tooltip on hover)\n          - Confidence score distribution for predictions on current image\n          - Navigation buttons (previous/next image) for sequential viewing\n        </per_image_statistics>\n      </right_panel>\n    </image_comparison_view>\n\n    <navigation>\n      - Top navigation bar with links to Statistics Dashboard and Image Comparison View\n      - Active page indicator in navigation bar\n      - Breadcrumb navigation for context (current dataset path, current image)\n      - Back to top button for long pages (statistics dashboard)\n      - Responsive navigation (collapsible menu on mobile devices)\n    </navigation>\n\n    <error_handling>\n      - User-friendly error messages for invalid dataset paths\n      - Validation errors for malformed JSON files (line number + error description)\n      - Warning messages for mismatched filenames (GT/prediction JSON without corresponding image)\n      - Loading spinners during data processing/file parsing\n      - Empty state handling (no data loaded, no images to display)\n      - Fallback UI for unsupported image formats\n    </error_handling>\n\n    <accessibility>\n      - Keyboard navigation (Tab/Enter for list selection, arrow keys for image navigation)\n      - Alt text for all images and icons\n      - High contrast mode for bounding boxes (optional toggle)\n      - Screen reader compatible labels for all UI elements\n      - Responsive design for mobile/tablet/desktop viewing\n      - Text size adjustment option (small/medium/large)\n    </accessibility>\n  </core_features>\n\n  <database_schema>\n    <tables>\n      <dataset_metadata>\n        - id (primary key, integer)\n        - path (text, unique)\n        - total_images (integer)\n        - total_classes (integer)\n        - iou_threshold (float, default 0.5)\n        - confidence_threshold (float, default 0.5)\n        - created_at (timestamp)\n        - last_updated (timestamp)\n      </dataset_metadata>\n\n      <image_metadata>\n        - id (primary key, integer)\n        - dataset_id (foreign key to dataset_metadata.id)\n        - filename (text)\n        - width (integer)\n        - height (integer)\n        - thumbnail_path (text)\n        - total_gt_boxes (integer)\n        - total_pred_boxes (integer)\n        - has_fp (boolean)\n        - has_fn (boolean)\n        - is_perfect (boolean)\n      </image_metadata>\n\n      <classes>\n        - id (primary key, integer)\n        - dataset_id (foreign key to dataset_metadata.id)\n        - name (text, unique per dataset)\n        - total_gt_count (integer)\n        - total_pred_count (integer)\n        - tp_count (integer)\n        - fp_count (integer)\n        - fn_count (integer)\n        - recall (float)\n        - precision (float)\n        - fpr (float)\n        - f1_score (float)\n      </classes>\n\n      <bounding_boxes>\n        - id (primary key, integer)\n        - image_id (foreign key to image_metadata.id)\n        - class_id (foreign key to classes.id)\n        - type (text, enum: 'ground_truth', 'prediction')\n        - x1 (float)\n        - y1 (float)\n        - x2 (float)\n        - y2 (float)\n        - confidence (float, null for ground truth)\n        - iou (float, null for unmatched boxes)\n        - classification (text, enum: 'tp', 'fp', 'fn', null for unclassified)\n      </bounding_boxes>\n    </tables>\n    <notes>\n      - Database is SQLite (file-based) for simplicity, stored as dataset_analysis.db\n      - Data is cleared/overwritten when a new dataset is loaded\n      - Indexes on filename, class name, and image_id for faster queries\n    </notes>\n  </database_schema>\n\n  <api_endpoints_summary>\n    <dataset>\n      - POST /api/dataset/load: Load and parse dataset from provided path\n        - Request body: { \"dataset_path\": \"/path/to/dataset\", \"iou_threshold\": 0.5 }\n        - Response: { \"success\": true, \"dataset_id\": 1, \"total_images\": 100, \"total_classes\": 5, \"errors\": [] }\n      - GET /api/dataset/metadata/:id: Get dataset metadata and summary statistics\n      - DELETE /api/dataset/:id: Clear dataset from memory/database\n    </dataset>\n\n    <statistics>\n      - GET /api/statistics/:dataset_id: Get all per-class statistics\n        - Response: { \"classes\": [...], \"overall_metrics\": {...}, \"iou_threshold\": 0.5 }\n      - POST /api/statistics/recalculate: Recalculate metrics with new thresholds\n        - Request body: { \"dataset_id\": 1, \"iou_threshold\": 0.6, \"confidence_threshold\": 0.7 }\n        - Response: { \"success\": true, \"statistics\": {...} }\n      - GET /api/statistics/export/:dataset_id: Export statistics to CSV/JSON\n        - Query params: { \"format\": \"csv\" }\n    </statistics>\n\n    <images>\n      -
